# Entropy III Multiplayer Protoss Scripts
# Courtesy of Broodwarai.com
# To be used with the BWAI Launcher
#=========================
#Script IDs-- For quick search just search for #scriptid; 
#searching for #unlp would take you to the Unleaded Protoss section
#=========================
#ASHP: Ashara Protoss
#mykp: Myk Protoss
#pabp: Panda Protoss
#PEPP: Peppe Protoss
#RACP: Racine Protoss
#RAYP: Raynor Protoss
#relp: Relentless Protoss
#unlp: Unleaded Protoss
#ZLDP: Zelduck Protoss
# stat_txt.tbl entry 1343: Protoss Expansion Custom Level<0>
PMCx(1343, 101, bwscript):
	start_town()
	transports_off()
	farms_notiming()
	groundmap_jump(PMCx 0000)
	#Island Scripts
	random_jump(128, rocp:null)
	goto(unlp:null)

#Random Script Selection
		--PMCx 0000--
	race_jump(pvtp, pvz, pvtp)
#vs terran and protoss
    --pvtp--
	random_jump(28, relp:null)
	random_jump(32, rocp:null)
	random_jump(36, ASHP:null)
	random_jump(42, RAYP:null)
	random_jump(50, mykp:null)
	random_jump(64, unlp:null)
	random_jump(84, RACP:null)
	random_jump(128, PEPP:null)
	goto(ZLDP:null)
#vs zerg
	--pvz--
	random_jump(28, relp:null)
	random_jump(32, rocp:null)
	random_jump(36, ASHP:null)
	random_jump(42, RAYP:null)
	random_jump(50, mykp:null)
	random_jump(64, pabp:null)
	random_jump(84, unlp:null)
	random_jump(128, PEPP:null)
	goto(ZLDP:null)

################Ashara Protoss######################

	# stat_txt.tbl entry 1343: Protoss Expansion Custom Level<0>
mykp(1343, 101, bwscript):
	start_town()
	transports_off()
	farms_notiming()
		--null--
	race_jump(PvT, PvZ, PvT)
--PvT--
	define_max(2, Protoss Shuttle)
	define_max(3, Protoss Observer)
	define_max(100, Protoss Zealot)
	define_max(100, Protoss Dragoon)
	define_max(2, Protoss High Templar)
	define_max(255, Protoss Dark Templar)
	define_max(255, Protoss Archon)
	define_max(255, Protoss Corsair)
	define_max(255, Protoss Dark Archon)
	define_max(255, Protoss Reaver)
	define_max(255, Protoss Carrier)
	define_max(255, Protoss Arbiter)
	define_max(255, Protoss Scout)
	build(1, Protoss Nexus, 150)
	build(8, Protoss Probe, 80)
	wait_buildstart(8, Protoss Probe)
	build(1, Protoss Pylon, 80)
	multirun(b_probes)
	wait_buildstart(10, Protoss Probe)
	build(1, Protoss Gateway, 80)
	wait_buildstart(12, Protoss Probe)
	build(1, Protoss Assimilator, 80)
	wait_buildstart(13, Protoss Probe)
	build(1, Protoss Cybernetics Core, 80)
	farms_timing()
	multirun(give_the_money)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Cybernetics Core)
	train(1, Protoss Dragoon)
	multirun(r_goon_range)
	multirun(t_dragoon)
	build(1, Protoss Robotics Facility, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Robotics Facility)
	build(1, Protoss Observatory, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Observatory)
	multirun(t_obs_2)
	expand(99, pvt_nat_expo)
	multirun(more_gates)
	build(1, Protoss Citadel of Adun, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Citadel of Adun)
	multirun(r_legspeed)
	multirun(t_zealot)
	build(1, Protoss Templar Archives, 80)
	multirun(r_templar)
	multirun(t_2_ht)
	build(1, Protoss Stargate, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Stargate)
	build(1, Protoss Fleet Beacon, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Fleet Beacon)
	multirun(pvt_expandmore)
	multirun(for_aiur)
	enemyowns_jump(Protoss Nexus, PvT_A)
	random_jump(128, PvT_A)
	goto(PvT_B)
		--PvT_A--
	multirun(t_zealot)
	multirun(t_dragoon)
	multirun(t_2_ht)
	define_max(8, Protoss Arbiter)
	build(1, Protoss Arbiter Tribunal, 80)
	wait_build(1, Protoss Arbiter Tribunal)
	multirun(t_arbiter)
	multirun(r_arbiterz)
	build(2, Protoss Stargate, 80)
	wait_build(2, Protoss Stargate)
	wait_train(1, Protoss Arbiter)
		--pvt_a_endloop--
	multirun(for_aiur)
	wait(100)
	multirun(t_zealot)
	multirun(t_dragoon)
	multirun(t_arbiter)
	multirun(t_2_ht)
	wait(3500)
	goto(pvt_a_endloop)
		--PvT_B--
	multirun(t_zealot)
	multirun(t_dragoon)
	multirun(t_2_ht)
	define_max(12, Protoss Carrier)
	multirun(r_core_airups)
	multirun(r_carrier_cap)
	build(3, Protoss Stargate, 80)
	wait_build(3, Protoss Stargate)
		--pvt_b_endloop--
	multirun(for_aiur)
	wait(100)
	multirun(t_zealot)
	multirun(t_dragoon)
	multirun(t_carrier)
	multirun(t_2_ht)
	wait(3500)
	goto(pvt_b_endloop)
	
#===PvZ===

    multirun(use_air)
    random_jump(64, DT_Rush)
    random_jump(128, DG_Rush)
    random_jump(128, ZL_Rush)
